 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">September&nbsp;22, 2021 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GENERAL MILLS REPORTS FISCAL 2022 FIRST-QUARTER RESULTS </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales increased 4&nbsp;percent to $4.5&nbsp;billion; organic net sales<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> were up 2&nbsp;percent </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit declined 1&nbsp;percent to $844&nbsp;million; constant-currency adjusted operating profit was
down 2&nbsp;percent </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted earnings per share (EPS) totaled $1.02, down 1&nbsp;percent from the prior year; adjusted diluted EPS
of $0.99 was down 2&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Company reaffirms full-year fiscal 2022 outlook </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&sup1;</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Please see Note 7 to the Consolidated Financial Statements below for reconciliation of this and other <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used in this release.</I> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">MINNEAPOLIS, Minn. &#150;
September&nbsp;22, 2021 &#150; General Mills (NYSE: GIS) today reported results for the first quarter ended August&nbsp;29, 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;I&#146;m proud of the way our team is performing in a dynamic and challenging operating environment,&#148; said General Mills Chairman
and Chief Executive Officer Jeff Harmening. &#147;Our strong execution in the first quarter enabled us to deliver <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-</FONT> and bottom-line results ahead of our expectations. We delivered these good results while
continuing to advance our Accelerate strategy, including making important progress on portfolio reshaping in the quarter.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General
Mills is executing its Accelerate strategy to drive sustainable, profitable growth and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> shareholder returns over the long term. The strategy focuses on four pillars to create competitive advantages and
win: boldly building brands, relentlessly innovating, unleashing scale, and being a force for good. The company is prioritizing its core markets, global platforms, and local gem brands that have the best prospects for profitable growth and is
committed to reshaping its portfolio with strategic acquisitions and divestitures, including the acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business and the planned divestiture of its European Yoplait operations, to further enhance its growth
profile. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills expects changes in consumer behaviors driven by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic will
result in ongoing elevated consumer demand for food at home, relative to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels. These changes include more time spent working from home and increased consumer appreciation for cooking and baking.
In addition, an increase in the pet population and further humanization and premiumization of pet food during the pandemic are expected to create tailwinds for the pet food category. The company plans to capitalize on these opportunities, addressing
evolving consumer needs through its leading brands, innovation, and advantaged capabilities to generate profitable growth. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>First Quarter Results
Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 4&nbsp;percent to $4.5&nbsp;billion, including 1 point of favorable foreign currency
exchange. Organic net sales increased 2&nbsp;percent, including contributions from positive organic net price realization and mix and higher organic pound volume. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was down 120 basis points to 35.2&nbsp;percent of net sales, primarily driven by higher input
costs, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects. Adjusted gross margin was down 150 basis points to 34.7&nbsp;percent of
net sales, driven by input cost inflation, higher other supply chain costs, and fixed cost deleverage in the supply chain, partially offset by Holistic Margin Management (HMM) cost savings and favorable net price realization and mix.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $844&nbsp;million was down 1&nbsp;percent, primarily driven by the comparison to net
gains on certain corporate investments in the prior year, partially offset by higher gross profit dollars<B>. Operating profit margin</B> of 18.6&nbsp;percent was down 100 basis points. Constant-currency adjusted operating profit declined
2&nbsp;percent, driven by lower adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by lower administrative expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin decreased 110 basis points to 18.0&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> was down 2&nbsp;percent to $627&nbsp;million and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was down 1&nbsp;percent to $1.02, primarily reflecting lower operating profit. Adjusted diluted EPS of $0.99 was down 2&nbsp;percent in constant currency, primarily driven by lower adjusted operating profit. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Portfolio Reshaping </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills took important
steps to advance its portfolio reshaping efforts in the first quarter. On July&nbsp;6, the company completed the acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business, including the <I>Nudges</I>, <I>True Chews</I>, and <I>Top Chews</I> brands. The
acquisition strengthens the company&#146;s position as the leading natural pet food manufacturer in the $37&nbsp;billion U.S. pet food category. The company estimates the acquisition will add approximately 2 cents to fiscal 2022 adjusted diluted
EPS. In addition, on August&nbsp;27, General Mills signed a definitive agreement in relation to the previously announced divestiture of its European Yoplait operations. The divestiture is scheduled to close by the end of calendar 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Operating Segment Results </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Note: Tables may not
foot due to rounding. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="92%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">


<TR>

<TD WIDTH="72%"></TD>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="4%"></TD>
<TD></TD>
<TD></TD>
<TD></TD>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="4%"></TD>
<TD></TD>
<TD></TD>
<TD></TD>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="3%"></TD>
<TD></TD>
<TD></TD>
<TD></TD>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="3%"></TD>
<TD></TD>
<TD></TD>
<TD></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt">
<TD VALIGN="bottom" COLSPAN="16" NOWRAP ALIGN="center" STYLE="border-bottom:1.00pt solid #000000"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Components of Fiscal 2022 Reported Net

<TD>&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Retail Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net sales for General Mills&#146; North America Retail segment declined 3&nbsp;percent to $2.64&nbsp;billion, driven by lower <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">at-home</FONT> food demand and the comparison to the prior-year period when net sales benefited from retailers rebuilding inventory that had been drawn down at the onset of the pandemic. Organic net sales also were down
3&nbsp;percent. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, relative to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels, first-quarter organic net sales were up 5&nbsp;percent. Net sales
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
declined 7&nbsp;percent in U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking and 6&nbsp;percent in U.S. Cereal, and were up 3&nbsp;percent in U.S. Snacks and up 3&nbsp;percent in constant currency in Canada. U.S.
Yogurt net sales essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels. Segment operating profit of $618&nbsp;million was down 11&nbsp;percent as reported and down 12&nbsp;percent in constant currency, primarily driven by
higher input costs and lower volume, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and lower administrative expenses. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, segment operating profit was up
4&nbsp;percent in constant currency. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Pet Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net sales for the Pet segment increased 25&nbsp;percent to $488&nbsp;million, driven by strong volume growth and favorable net price realization
and mix. Net sales growth included 5 points of benefit from the acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business, which closed on July&nbsp;6 and is being accounted for on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-month</FONT> lag. Organic net sales
were up 20&nbsp;percent, including double-digit growth for both dog food and cat food. Organic net sales growth benefited from the comparison to the prior-year period that was negatively impacted by a reduction in
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">at-home</FONT> pet food inventory, and on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, first-quarter organic net sales were up 13&nbsp;percent. The Blue Buffalo brand continued to drive
strong retail sales growth and market share gains in measured channels in the quarter. In addition, retail sales for the recently acquired pet treat brands were up 20&nbsp;percent in measured channels. Segment operating profit increased
28&nbsp;percent to $115&nbsp;million, primarily driven by favorable net price realization and mix and higher volume, partially offset by higher input costs and higher selling, general, and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses. On a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, segment operating profit was up 20&nbsp;percent in constant currency. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Convenience
Stores&nbsp;&amp; Foodservice Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net sales for the Convenience Stores&nbsp;&amp; Foodservice segment increased 23&nbsp;percent to
$482&nbsp;million, reflecting sequential recovery in key away-from-home food channels including schools, restaurants, lodging, and convenience stores. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, relative to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels, first-quarter organic net sales were up 4&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 47&nbsp;percent to $102&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and higher
volume, partially offset by higher input costs. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, segment operating profit was up 6&nbsp;percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Europe&nbsp;&amp; Australia Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net
sales for the Europe&nbsp;&amp; Australia segment increased 5&nbsp;percent to $518&nbsp;million, driven by favorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels. On a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, relative to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels, first-quarter organic net sales were up 3&nbsp;percent. Net sales growth for snack bars and yogurt was offset by
a decline in ice cream. Segment operating profit of $45&nbsp;million was down 15&nbsp;percent as reported and down 22&nbsp;percent in constant currency, primarily driven by input cost inflation and unfavorable product mix, partially offset by HMM
cost savings. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, segment operating profit was up 21&nbsp;percent in constant currency. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Asia&nbsp;&amp; Latin America Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net
sales for the Asia&nbsp;&amp; Latin America segment increased 8&nbsp;percent to $413&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and foreign currency exchange, partially offset by lower volume. Organic net sales increased
6&nbsp;percent. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, relative to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels, first-quarter organic net sales were up 11&nbsp;percent. Net sales performance was
led by <I>Yoki</I> meals and snacks in Brazil and <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream in China. Segment operating profit of $15&nbsp;million was down 23&nbsp;percent as reported and down 26&nbsp;percent in
constant currency, primarily driven by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, segment operating profit
was up 11&nbsp;percent in constant currency. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Venture Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First-quarter net sales for Cereal Partners Worldwide (CPW) were down 5&nbsp;percent in constant currency, reflecting the comparison against elevated demand
for food at home a year ago in the early stages of the pandemic. Constant-currency net sales increased 14&nbsp;percent for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT> Japan (HDJ), driven by strong new product performance. Combined <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures totaled $29&nbsp;million compared to $41&nbsp;million a year ago, primarily driven by lower net sales and higher media investment at CPW. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Other Income Statement Items </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated corporate items totaled $56&nbsp;million net expense in the first quarter of fiscal 2022, compared to $74&nbsp;million net expense a year ago.
Excluding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation effects and other items affecting comparability, unallocated corporate items totaled $77&nbsp;million net expense this year compared
to $96&nbsp;million net expense last year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring, impairment, and other exit costs totaled a $4&nbsp;million net recovery in the
quarter and were an insignificant amount a year ago <I>(please see Note 3 below for more information on these charges)</I>. <I></I> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net
interest expense totaled $96&nbsp;million in the first quarter compared to $111&nbsp;million a year ago, primarily driven by lower rates and lower average debt balances. The effective tax rate in the quarter was 21.7&nbsp;percent compared to
22.0&nbsp;percent last year <I>(please see Note 6 below for more information on our effective tax rate)</I>. The adjusted effective tax rate was 21.7&nbsp;percent compared to 21.9&nbsp;percent a year ago. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Cash Flow Generation and Cash Returns </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash
provided by operating activities totaled $370&nbsp;million in the first quarter of fiscal 2022 compared to $584&nbsp;million in the prior year, primarily driven by timing-related changes in accounts payable and accounts receivable. Capital
investments totaled $104&nbsp;million compared to $117&nbsp;million a year ago. Dividends paid increased to $312&nbsp;million. General Mills repurchased approximately 2.5&nbsp;million shares of common stock in the first quarter for a total of
$150&nbsp;million. Average diluted shares outstanding decreased 1&nbsp;percent to 615&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fiscal 2022 Outlook </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills reaffirmed its key full-year fiscal 2022 targets: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Organic net sales</B> are expected to be toward the higher end of the company&#146;s initial guidance range of
down 1 to 3&nbsp;percent, reflecting stronger-than-expected net sales performance in the first quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Constant-currency<B> adjusted operating profit</B> and constant-currency <B>adjusted diluted EPS</B> are each
expected to be toward the higher end of the company&#146;s initial guidance ranges of down 2 to 4&nbsp;percent and flat to down 2&nbsp;percent, respectively, largely due to the impact of the pet treats acquisition, which is estimated to add
approximately 2 cents to fiscal 2022 adjusted diluted EPS. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Free cash flow conversion </B>is expected to be approximately 95&nbsp;percent of adjusted <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">The above targets exclude the impact of the European Yoplait divestiture, which is scheduled to close by the end
of the calendar year. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills will issue <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-recorded</FONT> management remarks today,
September&nbsp;22, 2021, at approximately 6:30 a.m. Central time (7:30 a.m. Eastern time) and will hold a live, webcasted question and answer session beginning at 8:00 a.m. Central time (9:00 a.m. Eastern time). The
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-recorded</FONT> remarks and the webcast will be made available at <U>www.generalmills.com/investors</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This press
release contains forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995 that are based on our current expectations and assumptions. These forward-looking statements, including the statements under the
caption &#147;Fiscal 2022 Outlook,&#148; and statements made by Mr.&nbsp;Harmening, are subject to certain risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from the potential results discussed in the forward-looking
statements. In particular, our predictions about future net sales and earnings could be affected by a variety of factors, including: the impact of the coronavirus <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(COVID-19)</FONT> pandemic on our business,
suppliers, consumers, customers, and employees; disruptions or inefficiencies in the supply chain, including any impact of the coronavirus <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(COVID-19)</FONT> pandemic; competitive dynamics in the consumer foods
industry and the markets for our products, including new product introductions, advertising activities, pricing actions, and promotional activities of our competitors; economic conditions, including changes in inflation rates, interest rates, tax
rates, or the availability of capital; product development and innovation; consumer acceptance of new products and product improvements; consumer reaction to pricing actions and changes in promotion levels; acquisitions or dispositions of businesses
or assets; changes in capital structure; changes in the legal and regulatory environment, including tax legislation, labeling and advertising regulations, and litigation; impairments in the carrying value of goodwill, other intangible assets, or
other long-lived assets, or changes in the useful lives of other intangible assets; changes in accounting standards and the impact of significant accounting estimates; product quality and safety issues, including recalls and product liability;
changes in consumer demand for our products; effectiveness of advertising, marketing, and promotional programs; changes in consumer behavior, trends, and preferences, including weight loss trends; consumer perception of health-related issues,
including obesity; consolidation in the retail environment; changes in purchasing and inventory levels of significant customers; fluctuations in the cost and availability of supply chain resources, including raw materials, packaging, energy, and
transportation; effectiveness of restructuring and cost saving initiatives; volatility in the market value of derivatives used to manage price risk for certain commodities; benefit plan expenses due to changes in plan asset values and discount rates

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">GENERAL MILLS, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(Unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The accompanying Consolidated Financial Statements of General Mills, Inc. (we, us, our, General Mills, or the
Company) have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States for annual and interim financial information. In the opinion of management, all adjustments considered necessary for a fair presentation
have been included and are of a normal recurring nature. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the first quarter of fiscal 2022, we acquired the Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business for
$1.2&nbsp;billion in cash. We financed the transaction with a combination of cash on hand and short-term debt. We consolidated the Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business into our Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $759&nbsp;million,
indefinite-lived intangible assets for the <I>Nudges</I>, <I>Top Chews</I> and <I>True Chews</I> brands totaling $330&nbsp;million in aggregate, and a finite-lived customer relationship asset of $40&nbsp;million. We recorded acquisition integration
costs of $12&nbsp;million in the first quarter of fiscal 2022. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of fiscal 2022, we entered into
a definitive agreement to sell our 51&nbsp;percent controlling interest in Yoplait SAS, and our 50&nbsp;percent interest in Yoplait Marques SNC and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl to Sodiaal International (Sodiaal) in exchange for full ownership
of the Canadian Yoplait business, a reduced royalty rate for the use of Yoplait and Libert&eacute; brands in the United States and Canada, and cash. This transaction is expected to be completed by the end of calendar year 2021. We have reclassified
all Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl assets and liabilities as held for sale as of August&nbsp;29, 2021. We recorded transaction costs of $11&nbsp;million in the first quarter of fiscal 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$74&nbsp;million in the same period in fiscal 2021. We recorded a $24&nbsp;million net decrease in expense related to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity
positions and grain inventories in the first quarter of fiscal 2022 compared to a $16&nbsp;million net decrease in expense in the same period last year. We recorded $1&nbsp;million of net losses related to valuation adjustments on certain corporate
investments in the first quarter of fiscal 2022 compared to $13&nbsp;million of net gains related to valuation adjustments in the first quarter of fiscal 2021. In addition, we recorded $12&nbsp;million of integration costs related to our acquisition
of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business and $11&nbsp;million of transaction costs related to the agreement to sell our 51&nbsp;percent controlling interest in Yoplait SAS and our 50&nbsp;percent interest in Yoplait Marques SNC and Libert&eacute;
Marques S&agrave;rl in the first quarter of fiscal 2022. We also recorded a $21&nbsp;million recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item&nbsp;and a $13&nbsp;million insurance recovery in the first quarter of fiscal 2022. In the first quarter of
fiscal 2021, we recorded a $7&nbsp;million charge related to a product recall in our international Green Giant business. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(6)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The effective tax rate for the first quarter of fiscal 2022 was 21.7&nbsp;percent compared to 22.0&nbsp;percent
for the first quarter of fiscal 2021. The 0.3 percentage point decrease was primarily due to favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction. Our adjusted effective tax rate was 21.7&nbsp;percent in the first quarter of fiscal 2022 compared to
21.9&nbsp;percent in the same period last year (see Note 7 below for a description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 0.2 percentage point decrease in the adjusted effective tax rate was primarily due to favorable changes in earnings
mix by jurisdiction. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The United States Congress is currently working to enact a tax reform bill, which would result in
significant changes to the U.S. tax system. We expect that if a bill is enacted, it could have a material impact on our Consolidated Financial Statements in future periods. We continue to monitor developments and assess the impact to General Mills.
</P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(7)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">We have included measures in this release that are not defined by GAAP. We believe that these measures provide
useful information to investors, and include these measures in other communications to investors. For each of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, we are providing below a reconciliation of the differences
between the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure and the most directly comparable GAAP measure, an explanation of why we believe the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure provides useful information to
investors and any additional material purposes for which our management or Board of Directors uses the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure. These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures should be viewed in
addition to, and not in lieu of, the comparable GAAP measure. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We provide organic net sales growth rates for our
consolidated net sales and segment net sales. This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the Board of Directors&#146; measurement of our performance for incentive compensation purposes.
We believe that organic net sales growth rates provide useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance in our net sales by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations,
acquisitions, divestitures, and a 53rd&nbsp;fiscal week, when applicable, have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability. A reconciliation of these measures to reported net sales
growth rates, the relevant GAAP measures, are included in our Operating Segment Results above. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain measures in this release are
presented excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange (constant-currency). To present this information, current period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are translated into United States dollars at
the average exchange rates in effect during the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year, rather than the actual average exchange rates in effect during the current fiscal year. Therefore, the foreign currency impact is equal to current year
results in local currencies multiplied by the change in the average foreign currency exchange rate between the current fiscal period and the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year. We believe that these constant-currency measures provide
useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Also, certain measures in this release are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently
occurring events or items that, in management&#146;s judgment, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2022 outlook for organic net sales growth, adjusted operating profit growth, adjusted diluted EPS growth, and free cash flow
conversion are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude, or have otherwise been adjusted for, items impacting comparability, including the effect of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions,
divestitures, and a 53rd week, when applicable. We are not able to reconcile these forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to their most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure without
unreasonable efforts because we are unable to predict with a reasonable degree of certainty the actual impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates or the timing of acquisitions and divestitures throughout fiscal 2022. The unavailable
information could have a significant impact on our fiscal 2022 GAAP financial results. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2022 guidance does not incorporate the potential impact of the European Yoplait
divestiture that has not yet been completed. For fiscal 2022, we currently expect: foreign currency exchange rates (based on a blend of forward and forecasted rates and hedge positions) and acquisitions and divestitures to increase net sales by
approximately 2 points; foreign currency exchange rates to have an immaterial impact on adjusted operating profit and adjusted diluted EPS growth; and restructuring charges and project-related costs related to actions previously announced and
transaction costs and acquisition integration costs to total approximately $50&nbsp;million to $100&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Significant Items Impacting
Comparability </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Several measures below are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring
events or items that, in management&#146;s judgement, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are descriptions of significant items impacting comparability of our results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions
recognized in unallocated corporate items. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-income</FONT> tax recovery</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item recorded in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Acquisition integration costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Integration costs resulting from the acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business. Please see Note 2. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Transaction costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Transaction costs related to the definitive agreement to sell our 51&nbsp;percent controlling interest in Yoplait SAS, and our 50&nbsp;percent
interest in Yoplait Marques SNC and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl to Sodiaal. Please see Note 2. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Restructuring charges</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges for previously announced restructuring actions. Please see Note 3. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Investment activity, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Valuation adjustments of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2022 and fiscal 2021. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product recall</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Product
recall costs recorded in fiscal 2021 related to our international Green Giant business. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>CPW restructuring
charges</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CPW restructuring charges related to previously announced restructuring actions. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Operating Profit Growth on a Constant-currency Basis </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the measurement of our performance for incentive

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. The measure is evaluated on a constant-currency basis by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given the volatility in foreign currency exchange rates. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our adjusted operating

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Constant-currency Segment Operating Profit Growth Rates </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it provides transparency to underlying performance of our segments by excluding
the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Effective Income Tax Rate </U></P>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted effective income tax rates are calculated as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
